  258 | const stats = computed(() => {
  259 |   const result = { online: 0, offline: 0, alert: 0 }
  260 |   lights.value.forEach(light => {
  261 |     if (light.status === 'offline') result.offline++
  262 |     else if (light.status === 'alert') result.alert++
  263 |     else result.online++
  264 |   })
  265 |   return result
  266 | })

  268 | const filteredLights = computed(() => {
  269 |   if (!searchText.value) {
  270 |     if (statusFilter.value === 'all') return lights.value
  271 |     return lights.value.filter(l => l.status.startsWith(statusFilter.value))
  272 |   }
  273 |   return lights.value.filter(l => 
  274 |     l.name.includes(searchText.value) || l.imei.includes(searchText.value)
  275 |   )
  276 | })

  281 |     'online-off': 'light-off',
  282 |     'alert': 'light-alert',
  283 |     'offline': 'light-offline'
  284 |   }
  285 |   return classMap[status] || ''
  286 | }
  287 | 
  288 | const getLightPosition = (index) => {

  291 |     return { left: light.x + '%', top: light.y + '%' }
  292 |   }
  293 |   return {}

  328 |     } else {
  329 |       selectedLight.value.status = 'online-off'
  330 |     }
  331 |   }
  332 |   showBrightness.value = false
  333 | }
  334 | 
  335 | const batchControl = (action) => {
  336 |   lights.value.forEach(light => {
  337 |     if (light.status !== 'offline') {
  338 |       if (action === 'on') {
  339 |         light.status = 'online-on'
  340 |       } else {
  341 |         light.status = 'online-off'
  342 |       }
  343 |     }
  344 |   })
  345 | }

  365 | const availableLamps = computed(() => {
  366 |   let result = allLamps.value.filter(l => !selectedLampIds.value.includes(l.id))
  367 |   if (leftSearch.value) {
  368 |     result = result.filter(l => l.name.includes(leftSearch.value) || l.code.includes(leftSearch.value))
  369 |   }
  370 |   return result
  371 | })
  372 | 
  373 | const selectedLamps = computed(() => {
  374 |   let result = allLamps.value.filter(l => selectedLampIds.value.includes(l.id))
  375 |   if (rightSearch.value) {
  376 |     result = result.filter(l => l.name.includes(rightSearch.value) || l.code.includes(rightSearch.value))
  377 |   }
  378 |   return result
  379 | })
  380 | 
  381 | const filteredGroups = computed(() => {
  382 |   let result = groups.value
  383 |   if (filters.search) {
  384 |     result = result.filter(g => g.name.includes(filters.search))
  385 |   }
  386 |   if (filters.type) {
  387 |     result = result.filter(g => g.type === filters.type)
  388 |   }
  389 |   if (filters.hierarchy) {
  390 |     result = result.filter(g => g.hierarchy === filters.hierarchy)
  391 |   }
  392 |   return result
  393 | })
  394 | 
  395 | const getTypeText = (type) => {
  396 |   const map = { road: '路段分组', function: '功能分组', custom: '自定义分组' }
  397 |   return map[type] || type
  398 | }
  399 | 
  400 | const getTypeTagType = (type) => {
  401 |   const map = { road: 'primary', function: 'success', custom: 'warning' }
  402 |   return map[type] || ''
  403 | }
  404 | 
  405 | const getHierarchyText = (hierarchy) => {
  406 |   const map = { xiandao: '长沙-岳麓区-梅溪湖隧道', liwei: '长沙-岳麓区-梅溪湖隧道1栋' }
  407 |   return map[hierarchy] || hierarchy
  408 | }

  410 | const handleCheckChange = () => {}
  411 | 
  412 | const handleSelectionChange = (selection) => {
  413 |   selectedRows.value = selection
  414 | }
  415 | 
  416 | const searchGroups = () => {
  417 |   currentPage.value = 1
  418 |   ElMessage.success('查询成功')
  419 | }
  420 | 
  421 | const resetFilters = () => {
  422 |   Object.assign(filters, { search: '', type: '', hierarchy: '' })
  423 |   currentPage.value = 1
  424 | }
  425 | 
  426 | const refreshData = () => {
  427 |   ElMessage.success('数据已刷新')
  428 | }
  429 | 
  430 | const handleExport = () => {
  431 |   ElMessage.success('导出成功')
  432 | }
  433 | 
  434 | const batchDelete = () => {
  435 |   ElMessageBox.confirm(`确定要删除选中的${selectedRows.value.length}个分组吗？`, '提示', {
  436 |     confirmButtonText: '确定',
  437 |     cancelButtonText: '取消',
  438 |     type: 'warning'
  439 |   }).then(() => {
  440 |     const selectedIds = selectedRows.value.map(g => g.id)
  441 |     groups.value = groups.value.filter(g => !selectedIds.includes(g.id))
  442 |     total.value = groups.value.length
  443 |     selectedRows.value = []
  444 |     ElMessage.success('批量删除成功')
  445 |   }).catch(() => {})
  446 | }
  447 | 
  448 | const handleLeftSelection = (selection) => {
  449 |   tempLeftSelection.value = selection
  450 | }
  451 | 
  452 | const handleRightSelection = (selection) => {
  453 |   tempRightSelection.value = selection
  454 | }
  455 | 
  456 | const addSelectedLamps = () => {
  457 |   tempLeftSelection.value.forEach(item => {
  458 |     if (!selectedLampIds.value.includes(item.id)) {
  459 |       selectedLampIds.value.push(item.id)
  460 |     }
  461 |   })
  462 |   tempLeftSelection.value = []
  463 | }
  464 | 
  465 | const removeSelectedLamps = () => {
  466 |   tempRightSelection.value.forEach(item => {
  467 |     const index = selectedLampIds.value.indexOf(item.id)
  468 |     if (index > -1) {
  469 |       selectedLampIds.value.splice(index, 1)
  470 |     }
  471 |   })
  472 |   tempRightSelection.value = []
  473 | }
  474 | 
  475 | const searchLeftLamps = () => {}
  476 | const resetLeftSearch = () => { leftSearch.value = '' }
  477 | const searchRightLamps = () => {}
  478 | const resetRightSearch = () => { rightSearch.value = '' }
  479 | 
  480 | const resetForm = () => {
  481 |   Object.assign(form, { name: '', type: 'road', hierarchy: '', remark: '' })
  482 |   selectedLampIds.value = []
  483 |   tempLeftSelection.value = []
  484 |   tempRightSelection.value = []
  485 | }
  486 | 
  487 | const editGroup = (row) => {
  488 |   isEdit.value = true
  489 |   Object.assign(form, { name: row.name, type: row.type, hierarchy: row.hierarchy, remark: row.remark })
  490 |   selectedLampIds.value = [...(row.lampIds || [])]
  491 |   showAddDialog.value = true
  492 | }
  493 | 
  494 | const deleteGroup = (row) => {
  495 |   ElMessageBox.confirm(`确定要删除分组"${row.name}"吗？`, '提示', {
  496 |     confirmButtonText: '确定',
  497 |     cancelButtonText: '取消',
  498 |     type: 'warning'
  499 |   }).then(() => {
  500 |     const index = groups.value.findIndex(g => g.id === row.id)
  501 |     if (index > -1) {
  502 |       groups.value.splice(index, 1)
  503 |       total.value--
  504 |       ElMessage.success('删除成功')
  505 |     }
  506 |   }).catch(() => {})
  507 | }
  508 | 
  509 | const submitForm = () => {
  510 |   formRef.value.validate((valid) => {
  511 |     if (valid) {
  512 |       if (isEdit.value) {
  513 |         const index = groups.value.findIndex(g => g.id === form.id)
  514 |         if (index > -1) {
  515 |           groups.value[index] = {
  516 |             ...groups.value[index],
  517 |             ...form,
  518 |             lampCount: selectedLampIds.value.length,
  519 |             lampIds: [...selectedLampIds.value]
  520 |           }
  521 |         }
  522 |         ElMessage.success('分组修改成功')
  523 |       } else {
  524 |         const newId = Math.max(...groups.value.map(g => g.id)) + 1
  525 |         groups.value.push({
  526 |           id: newId,
  527 |           no: groups.value.length + 1,
  528 |           ...form,
  529 |           lampCount: selectedLampIds.value.length,
  530 |           lampIds: [...selectedLampIds.value],
  531 |           createTime: new Date().toLocaleString()
  532 |         })
  533 |         total.value++
  534 |         ElMessage.success('分组添加成功')
  535 |       }
  536 |       showAddDialog.value = false
  537 |       isEdit.value = false
  538 |       resetForm()
  539 |     }
  540 |   })
  541 | }
  542 | 
  543 | const viewLamps = (row) => {
  544 |   currentGroupLamps.value = allLamps.value.filter(l => row.lampIds?.includes(l.id))
  545 |   showLampListDialog.value = true
  546 | }
  547 | 
  548 | const showLampDialog = (row) => {
  549 |   viewLamps(row)
  550 | }
  551 | 
  552 | const batchControl = (row) => {
  553 |   showControlDialog.value = true
  554 | }
  555 | 
  556 | const submitControl = () => {
  557 |   const action = controlType.value === 'on' ? '开灯' : controlType.value === 'off' ? '关灯' : `调光至${brightnessValue.value}%`
  558 |   ElMessage.success(`批量${action}成功`)
  559 |   showControlDialog.value = false
  560 | }

  309 | const filteredRecords = computed(() => {
  310 |   let result = records.value
  311 |   if (filters.name) {
  312 |     result = result.filter(r => r.strategyName.includes(filters.name))
  313 |   }
  314 |   if (filters.status) {
  315 |     result = result.filter(r => r.status === filters.status)
  316 |   }
  317 |   return result
  318 | })
  319 | 
  320 | const getTypeText = (type) => {
  321 |   const map = { time: '定时策略', light: '光感策略', manual: '手动策略' }
  322 |   return map[type] || type
  323 | }
  324 | 
  325 | const getActionText = (action) => {
  326 |   const map = { on: '开灯', off: '关灯', dim: '调光' }
  327 |   return map[action] || action
  328 | }
  329 | 
  330 | const getStatusText = (status) => {
  331 |   const map = { success: '成功', partial: '部分成功', fail: '失败' }
  332 |   return map[status] || status
  333 | }
  334 | 
  335 | const getStatusTagType = (status) => {
  336 |   const map = { success: 'success', partial: 'warning', fail: 'danger' }
  337 |   return map[status] || ''
  338 | }
  339 | 
  340 | const handleSelectionChange = (selection) => {
  341 |   selectedRows.value = selection
  342 | }
  343 | 
  344 | const searchRecords = () => {
  345 |   currentPage.value = 1
  346 |   ElMessage.success('查询成功')
  347 | }
  348 |

  350 |   Object.assign(filters, {
  351 |     name: '',
  352 |     status: '',
  353 |     dateRange: []
  354 |   })
  355 |   currentPage.value = 1
  356 | }

  358 | const refreshData = () => {
  359 |   ElMessage.success('数据已刷新')
  360 | }
  361 | 
  362 | const viewDetail = (row) => {
  363 |   currentRecord.value = row
  364 |   detailVisible.value = true
  365 |   activeTab.value = 'config'
  366 | }
  367 | 
  368 | const handleCopy = (row) => {
  369 |   currentRecord.value = row
  370 |   Object.assign(copyForm, {
  371 |     originalName: row.strategyName,
  372 |     name: row.strategyName + ' (副本)',
  373 |     type: row.strategyType,
  374 |     executeTime: row.executeTime
  375 |   })
  376 |   copyVisible.value = true
  377 | }
  378 | 
  379 | const submitCopy = async () => {
  380 |   if (!copyFormRef.value) return
  381 |   await copyFormRef.value.validate((valid) => {
  382 |     if (valid) {
  383 |       ElMessage.success(`策略「${copyForm.name}」复制成功`)
  384 |       copyVisible.value = false
  385 |       router.push('/lighting/strategy')
  386 |     }
  387 |   })
  388 | }
  389 | 
  390 | const handleExportSingle = (row) => {
  391 |   ElMessage.success(`正在导出「${row.strategyName}」的执行记录...`)
  392 |   setTimeout(() => {
  393 |     ElMessage.success('导出成功，文件已开始下载')
  394 |   }, 500)
  395 | }
  396 | 
  397 | const handleExport = () => {
  398 |   ElMessageBox.confirm(`确定要导出选中的${selectedRows.value.length}条记录吗？`, '提示', {
  399 |     confirmButtonText: '确定',

  401 |     type: 'info'
  402 |   }).then(() => {

  404 |     setTimeout(() => {
  405 |       ElMessage.success('导出成功，Excel文件已开始下载')
  406 |     }, 500)
  407 |   }).catch(() => {})
  408 | }
  409 | 
  410 | const handleSizeChange = (val) => {
  411 |   pageSize.value = val
  412 | }
  413 | 
  414 | const handleCurrentChange = (val) => {
  415 |   currentPage.value = val
  416 | }

  244 | 
  245 | const filteredData = computed(() => {
  246 |   let result = lampData.value
  247 |   if (filterProduct.value) {
  248 |     result = result.filter(item => item.product === filterProduct.value)
  249 |   }
  250 |   if (filterLampStatus.value) {
  251 |     result = result.filter(item => item.lampStatus === filterLampStatus.value)
  252 |   }
  253 |   if (filterNetworkStatus.value) {
  254 |     result = result.filter(item => item.networkStatus === filterNetworkStatus.value)
  255 |   }
  256 |   if (filterEnabled.value) {
  257 |     result = result.filter(item => filterEnabled.value === 'enabled' ? item.enabled : !item.enabled)
  258 |   }
  259 |   if (searchKeyword.value) {
  260 |     result = result.filter(item => 
  261 |       item.imei.includes(searchKeyword.value) || 
  262 |       item.name.includes(searchKeyword.value)
  263 |     )
  264 |   }
  265 |   return result
  266 | })
  267 | 
  268 | const handleSelectionChange = (selection) => {
  269 |   selectedRows.value = selection
  270 | }
  271 | 
  272 | const handleSearch = () => {
  273 |   ElMessage.success('查询成功')
  274 | }
  275 | 
  276 | const handleReset = () => {
  277 |   searchKeyword.value = ''
  278 |   filterProduct.value = ''
  279 |   filterLampStatus.value = ''
  280 |   filterNetworkStatus.value = ''
  281 |   filterEnabled.value = ''
  282 | }
  283 | 
  284 | const handleTurnOn = () => {
  285 |   if (selectedRows.value.length === 0) {
  286 |     ElMessage.warning('请选择要控制的灯具')
  287 |     return
  288 |   }
  289 |   ElMessage.success(`已开启 ${selectedRows.value.length} 个灯具`)
  290 | }
  291 | 
  292 | const handleTurnOff = () => {
  293 |   if (selectedRows.value.length === 0) {
  294 |     ElMessage.warning('请选择要控制的灯具')
  295 |     return
  296 |   }
  297 |   ElMessage.success(`已关闭 ${selectedRows.value.length} 个灯具`)
  298 | }
  299 | 
  300 | const handleDimming = () => {
  301 |   if (selectedRows.value.length === 0) {
  302 |     ElMessage.warning('请选择要调光的灯具')
  303 |     return
  304 |   }
  305 |   ElMessage.success(`已将 ${selectedRows.value.length} 个灯具亮度设置为 ${brightnessValue.value}%`)
  306 |   showDimmingDialog.value = false
  307 | }
  308 | 
  309 | const handleDetail = (row) => {
  310 |   selectedItem.value = row
  311 |   showDetailDialog.value = true
  312 | }
  313 | 
  314 | const handleMore = (row) => {
  315 |   ElMessage.info(`更多操作: ${row.name}`)
  316 | }
  317 | 
  318 | const handleViewSwitchRecord = (row) => {
  319 |   ElMessage.info(`查看 ${row.name} 的开关灯记录`)
  320 | }

   52 |               />

   54 |             </div>

   56 |               <el-button v-for="level in brightnessLevels" :key="level" @click="setBrightness(level)">
   57 |                 {{ level }}%
   58 |               </el-button>
   59 |             </div>

   62 |       </div>

   72 |           <template #default="scope">
   73 |             <el-tag :type="getStatusTagType(scope.row.status)">
   74 |               {{ getStatusText(scope.row.status) }}
   75 |             </el-tag>

   82 |             <el-button

   84 |               :type="scope.row.status === 'on' ? 'default' : 'primary'"
   85 |               @click="toggleLight(scope.row)"
   86 |             >
   87 |               {{ scope.row.status === 'on' ? '关闭' : '开启' }}
   88 |             </el-button>

   90 |           </template>
   91 |         </el-table-column>

   96 |         <div class="light-info">{{ currentLight.name }}</div>
   97 |         <el-slider 
   98 |           v-model="currentBrightness" 
   99 |           :min="0" 
  100 |           :max="100" 
  101 |           :step="1"
  102 |           show-input
  103 |         />
  104 |       </div>

  106 |         <el-button @click="brightnessDialogVisible = false">取消</el-button>
  107 |         <el-button type="primary" @click="confirmBrightness">确认</el-button>
  108 |       </template>
  109 |     </el-dialog>
  110 |   </div>
  111 | </template>

  113 | <script setup>
  114 | import { ref, computed } from 'vue'
  115 | import { VideoPlay, VideoPause, Grid, MapLocation } from '@element-plus/icons-vue'
  116 | import { lightStatusData } from '@/data/mockData'
  117 | 
  118 | const icons = { Power: VideoPlay, PowerOff: VideoPause, Batch: Grid, MapPin: MapLocation }
  119 | const selectedArea = ref('all')
  120 | const brightnessValue = ref(80)
  121 | const brightnessDialogVisible = ref(false)
  122 | const currentLight = ref(null)
  123 | const currentBrightness = ref(80)
  124 | const selectedLights = ref([])
  125 | 
  126 | const areas = [
  127 |   { id: 'all', name: '全部区域', icon: MapLocation },
  128 |   { id: 'zhongshan', name: '中山路', icon: MapLocation },
  129 |   { id: 'renmin', name: '人民路', icon: MapLocation },
  130 |   { id: 'jiefang', name: '解放路', icon: MapLocation },
  131 |   { id: 'gongyuan', name: '公园路', icon: MapLocation },
  132 |   { id: 'wenhua', name: '文化路', icon: MapLocation }
  133 | ]
  134 | 
  135 | const brightnessLevels = [30, 50, 70, 85, 100]
  136 | 
  137 | const tableData = ref([...lightStatusData])
  138 | 
  139 | const filteredLights = computed(() => {
  140 |   if (selectedArea.value === 'all') return tableData.value
  141 |   const areaMap = {
  142 |     zhongshan: '中山路',
  143 |     renmin: '人民路',
  144 |     jiefang: '解放路',
  145 |     gongyuan: '公园路',
  146 |     wenhua: '文化路'
  147 |   }
  148 |   return tableData.value.filter(item => item.location.includes(areaMap[selectedArea.value]))
  149 | })
  150 | 
  151 | const getAreaCount = (areaId) => {
  152 |   if (areaId === 'all') return tableData.value.length
  153 |   const areaMap = {
  154 |     zhongshan: '中山路',
  155 |     renmin: '人民路',
  156 |     jiefang: '解放路',
  157 |     gongyuan: '公园路',
  158 |     wenhua: '文化路'
  159 |   }
  160 |   return tableData.value.filter(item => item.location.includes(areaMap[areaId])).length
  161 | }
  162 | 
  163 | const getStatusTagType = (status) => {
  164 |   switch (status) {
  165 |     case 'on': return 'success'
  166 |     case 'off': return 'info'
  167 |     case 'fault': return 'danger'
  168 |     default: return 'info'
  169 |   }
  170 | }
  171 | 
  172 | const getStatusText = (status) => {
  173 |   switch (status) {
  174 |     case 'on': return '开启'
  175 |     case 'off': return '关闭'
  176 |     case 'fault': return '故障'
  177 |     default: return status
  178 |   }
  179 | }
  180 | 
  181 | const selectArea = (areaId) => {
  182 |   selectedArea.value = areaId
  183 | }
  184 | 
  185 | const controlAll = (action) => {
  186 |   filteredLights.value.forEach(light => {
  187 |     if (light.status !== 'fault') {
  188 |       light.status = action
  189 |       light.brightness = action === 'on' ? brightnessValue.value : 0
  190 |     }
  191 |   })
  192 | }
  193 | 
  194 | const toggleLight = (row) => {
  195 |   if (row.status === 'fault') return
  196 |   row.status = row.status === 'on' ? 'off' : 'on'
  197 |   row.brightness = row.status === 'on' ? brightnessValue.value : 0
  198 | }
  199 | 
  200 | const onBrightnessChange = (val) => {
  201 |   filteredLights.value.forEach(light => {
  202 |     if (light.status === 'on') {
  203 |       light.brightness = val
  204 |     }
  205 |   })
  206 | }
  207 | 
  208 | const setBrightness = (level) => {
  209 |   brightnessValue.value = level
  210 |   onBrightnessChange(level)
  211 | }
  212 | 
  213 | const adjustBrightness = (row) => {
  214 |   if (row.status === 'fault') return
  215 |   currentLight.value = row
  216 |   currentBrightness.value = row.brightness
  217 |   brightnessDialogVisible.value = true
  218 | }
  219 | 
  220 | const confirmBrightness = () => {
  221 |   if (currentLight.value && currentLight.value.status !== 'fault') {
  222 |     currentLight.value.brightness = currentBrightness.value
  223 |     if (currentLight.value.status === 'off') {
  224 |       currentLight.value.status = 'on'
  225 |     }
  226 |   }
  227 |   brightnessDialogVisible.value = false
  228 | }
  229 | 
  230 | const batchControl = () => {
  231 |   selectedLights.value.forEach(id => {
  232 |     const light = tableData.value.find(l => l.id === id)
  233 |     if (light && light.status !== 'fault') {
  234 |       light.status = 'on'
  235 |       light.brightness = brightnessValue.value
  236 |     }
  237 |   })
  238 | }
  239 | </script>

   86 | <script setup>
   87 | import { ref, computed } from 'vue'
   88 | import { Refresh } from '@element-plus/icons-vue'
   89 | import { lightStatusData } from '@/data/mockData'
   90 | 
   91 | const icons = { Refresh }
   92 | const statusFilter = ref('')
   93 | const searchKeyword = ref('')
   94 | const detailDialogVisible = ref(false)
   95 | const selectedLight = ref(null)
   96 | 
   97 | const tableData = ref([...lightStatusData])
   98 | 
   99 | const totalCount = computed(() => tableData.value.length)
  100 | const onlineCount = computed(() => tableData.value.filter(item => item.status === 'on').length)
  101 | const offlineCount = computed(() => tableData.value.filter(item => item.status === 'off').length)
  102 | const faultCount = computed(() => tableData.value.filter(item => item.status === 'fault').length)
  103 | 
  104 | const filteredData = computed(() => {
  105 |   return tableData.value.filter(item => {
  106 |     const statusMatch = !statusFilter.value || item.status === statusFilter.value
  107 |     const keywordMatch = !searchKeyword.value || 
  108 |       item.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchKeyword.value.toLowerCase()) ||
  109 |       item.location.toLowerCase().includes(searchKeyword.value.toLowerCase())
  110 |     return statusMatch && keywordMatch
  111 |   })
  112 | })
  113 | 
  114 | const getStatusTagType = (status) => {
  115 |   switch (status) {
  116 |     case 'on': return 'success'
  117 |     case 'off': return 'info'

  126 |     case 'off': return '关闭'
  127 |     case 'fault': return '故障'
  128 |     default: return status
  129 |   }
  130 | }
  131 | 
  132 | const refreshData = () => {
  133 |   tableData.value = [...lightStatusData]
  134 | }
  135 | 
  136 | const viewDetail = (row) => {
  137 |   selectedLight.value = row
  138 |   detailDialogVisible.value = true
  139 | }
  140 | </script>

  189 | const filteredStrategies = computed(() => {
  190 |   let result = strategies.value
  191 |   if (filters.name) {
  192 |     result = result.filter(s => s.name.includes(filters.name))
  193 |   }
  194 |   if (filters.type) {
  195 |     result = result.filter(s => s.type === filters.type)
  196 |   }
  197 |   if (filters.status) {
  198 |     result = result.filter(s => s.status === filters.status)
  199 |   }
  200 |   return result
  201 | })

  203 | const getTypeText = (type) => {

  205 |   return map[type] || type
  206 | }

  265 | const handlePause = (row) => {
  266 |   ElMessageBox.confirm(`确定要暂停策略「${row.name}」吗？`, '提示', {
  267 |     confirmButtonText: '确定',
  268 |     cancelButtonText: '取消',
  269 |     type: 'warning'
  270 |   }).then(() => {
  271 |     row.status = 'paused'
  272 |     ElMessage.success(`策略「${row.name}」已暂停`)
  273 |   }).catch(() => {})

  276 | const handleBatchIssue = () => {
  277 |   const notIssuedCount = selectedRows.value.filter(r => r.status === 'not_issued').length
  278 |   if (notIssuedCount === 0) {
  279 |     ElMessage.warning('请选择未下发的策略')
  280 |     return
  281 |   }
  282 |   ElMessageBox.confirm(`确定要批量下发选中的 ${notIssuedCount} 个策略吗？`, '提示', {
  283 |     confirmButtonText: '确定',
  284 |     cancelButtonText: '取消',
  285 |     type: 'primary'
  286 |   }).then(() => {
  287 |     selectedRows.value.forEach(row => {
  288 |       if (row.status === 'not_issued') {
  289 |         row.status = 'issued'
  290 |       }
  291 |     })
  292 |     ElMessage.success(`已成功下发 ${notIssuedCount} 个策略`)
  293 |   }).catch(() => {})
  294 | }
  295 | 
  296 | const handleBatchPause = () => {
  297 |   const issuedCount = selectedRows.value.filter(r => r.status === 'issued').length
  298 |   if (issuedCount === 0) {
  299 |     ElMessage.warning('请选择已下发的策略')
  300 |     return
  301 |   }
  302 |   ElMessageBox.confirm(`确定要批量暂停选中的 ${issuedCount} 个策略吗？`, '提示', {
  303 |     confirmButtonText: '确定',
  304 |     cancelButtonText: '取消',
  305 |     type: 'warning'
  306 |   }).then(() => {
  307 |     selectedRows.value.forEach(row => {
  308 |       if (row.status === 'issued') {
  309 |         row.status = 'paused'
  310 |       }
  311 |     })
  312 |     ElMessage.success(`已成功暂停 ${issuedCount} 个策略`)
  313 |   }).catch(() => {})
  314 | }

   66 |           />

   70 |         <el-button @click="dialogVisible = false">取消</el-button>
   71 |         <el-button type="primary" @click="saveStrategy">保存</el-button>
   72 |       </template>
   73 |     </el-dialog>
   74 |   </div>
   75 | </template>
   76 | 
   77 | <script setup>
   78 | import { ref, computed } from 'vue'
   79 | import { Plus, Edit, Delete } from '@element-plus/icons-vue'
   80 | import { timingStrategies } from '@/data/mockData'
   81 | 
   82 | const icons = { Plus, Edit, Delete }
   83 | const strategyList = ref([...timingStrategies])
   84 | const dialogVisible = ref(false)
   85 | const isEdit = ref(false)
   86 | const formData = ref({
   87 |   id: '',
   88 |   name: '',
   89 |   startTime: '',
   90 |   endTime: '',
   91 |   brightness: 80,
   92 |   enabled: true,
   93 |   createTime: ''
   94 | })
   95 | 
   96 | const editDialogTitle = computed(() => isEdit.value ? '编辑策略' : '新增策略')
   97 | 
   98 | const addStrategy = () => {
   99 |   isEdit.value = false
  100 |   formData.value = {
  101 |     id: '',
  102 |     name: '',
  103 |     startTime: '',
  104 |     endTime: '',
  105 |     brightness: 80,
  106 |     enabled: true,
  107 |     createTime: ''
  108 |   }
  109 |   dialogVisible.value = true
  110 | }
  111 | 
  112 | const editStrategy = (row) => {
  113 |   isEdit.value = true
  114 |   formData.value = { ...row }
  115 |   dialogVisible.value = true
  116 | }
  117 | 
  118 | const deleteStrategy = (row) => {
  119 |   ElMessageBox.confirm(
  120 |     '确定要删除该策略吗？',
  121 |     '提示',
  122 |     {
  123 |       confirmButtonText: '确定',
  124 |       cancelButtonText: '取消',
  125 |       type: 'warning'
  126 |     }
  127 |   ).then(() => {
  128 |     const index = strategyList.value.findIndex(s => s.id === row.id)
  129 |     if (index > -1) {
  130 |       strategyList.value.splice(index, 1)
  131 |     }
  132 |     ElMessage.success('删除成功')
  133 |   }).catch(() => {
  134 |     ElMessage.info('已取消删除')
  135 |   })
  136 | }
  137 | 
  138 | const toggleEnable = (row) => {
  139 |   row.enabled = !row.enabled
  140 | }
  141 | 
  142 | const saveStrategy = () => {
  143 |   if (!formData.value.name || !formData.value.startTime || !formData.value.endTime) {
  144 |     ElMessage.warning('请填写完整信息')
  145 |     return
  146 |   }
  147 |   
  148 |   if (isEdit.value) {
  149 |     const index = strategyList.value.findIndex(s => s.id === formData.value.id)
  150 |     if (index > -1) {
  151 |       strategyList.value[index] = { ...formData.value }
  152 |     }
  153 |     ElMessage.success('修改成功')
  154 |   } else {
  155 |     const newId = 'T' + String(strategyList.value.length + 1).padStart(3, '0')
  156 |     strategyList.value.push({
  157 |       ...formData.value,
  158 |       id: newId,
  159 |       createTime: new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]
  160 |     })
  161 |     ElMessage.success('新增成功')
  162 |   }
  163 |   dialogVisible.value = false
  164 | }
  165 | </script>
  166 | 
  167 | <style scoped>
  168 | .data-table {
  169 |   width: 100%;
  170 | }
  171 | </style>
  172 |

    1 | <template>
    2 |   <div class="page-container">
    3 |     <div class="page-header">
    4 |       <div class="title">回路用电数据</div>
    5 |       <div class="header-actions">
    6 |         <el-select v-model="selectedBox" placeholder="选择配电箱" class="box-select">
    7 |           <el-option label="全部" value="" />
    8 |           <el-option v-for="box in boxes" :key="box.id" :label="box.name" :value="box.id" />
    9 |         </el-select>
   10 |       </div>
   11 |     </div>
   12 |     <div class="circuit-stats">
   13 |       <div class="stat-card">
   14 |         <div class="stat-icon">
   15 |           <component :is="icons.Electricity" />
   16 |         </div>
   17 |         <div class="stat-info">
   18 |           <span class="stat-value">{{ totalPower.toFixed(1) }} kW</span>
   19 |           <span class="stat-label">总功率</span>
   20 |         </div>
   21 |       </div>
   22 |       <div class="stat-card">
   23 |         <div class="stat-icon">
   24 |           <component :is="icons.Battery" />
   25 |         </div>
   26 |         <div class="stat-info">
   27 |           <span class="stat-value">{{ totalEnergy }} kWh</span>
   28 |           <span class="stat-label">总用电量</span>
   29 |         </div>
   30 |       </div>
   31 |       <div class="stat-card">
   32 |         <div class="stat-icon">
   33 |           <component :is="icons.Gauge" />
   34 |         </div>
   35 |         <div class="stat-info">
   36 |           <span class="stat-value">{{ avgPowerFactor.toFixed(2) }}</span>
   37 |           <span class="stat-label">平均功率因数</span>
   38 |         </div>
   39 |       </div>
   40 |     </div>
   41 |     <el-table :data="filteredCircuits" border class="data-table">
   42 |       <el-table-column prop="id" label="回路编号" width="100" />
   43 |       <el-table-column prop="name" label="回路名称" />
   44 |       <el-table-column prop="boxId" label="所属配电箱" width="120">
   45 |         <template #default="scope">
   46 |           {{ getBoxName(scope.row.boxId) }}
   47 |         </template>
   48 |       </el-table-column>
   49 |       <el-table-column prop="power" label="功率(W)" width="100" />
   50 |       <el-table-column prop="energy" label="用电量(kWh)" width="120" />
   51 |       <el-table-column prop="voltage" label="电压(V)" width="100" />
   52 |       <el-table-column prop="current" label="电流(A)" width="100" />
   53 |       <el-table-column prop="powerFactor" label="功率因数" width="100" />
   54 |       <el-table-column label="功率因数状态" width="120">
   55 |         <template #default="scope">
   56 |           <el-tag :type="getPowerFactorTag(scope.row.powerFactor)">
   57 |             {{ getPowerFactorText(scope.row.powerFactor) }}
   58 |           </el-tag>
   59 |         </template>
   60 |       </el-table-column>
   61 |     </el-table>
   62 |   </div>
   63 | </template>
   64 | 
   65 | <script setup>
   66 | import { ref, computed } from 'vue'
   67 | import { Lightning, Tools, Cpu } from '@element-plus/icons-vue'
   68 | import { circuitData, distributionBoxes } from '@/data/mockData'
   69 | 
   70 | const icons = { Electricity: Lightning, Battery: Tools, Gauge: Cpu }
   71 | const selectedBox = ref('')
   72 | const circuits = ref([...circuitData])
   73 | const boxes = ref([...distributionBoxes])
   74 | 
   75 | const filteredCircuits = computed(() => {
   76 |   if (!selectedBox.value) return circuits.value
   77 |   return circuits.value.filter(c => c.boxId === selectedBox.value)
   78 | })
   79 | 
   80 | const totalPower = computed(() => {
   81 |   return filteredCircuits.value.reduce((sum, c) => sum + c.power, 0) / 1000
   82 | })
   83 | 
   84 | const totalEnergy = computed(() => {
   85 |   return filteredCircuits.value.reduce((sum, c) => sum + c.energy, 0)
   86 | })
   87 | 
   88 | const avgPowerFactor = computed(() => {
   89 |   const count = filteredCircuits.value.length
   90 |   if (count === 0) return 0
   91 |   return filteredCircuits.value.reduce((sum, c) => sum + c.powerFactor, 0) / count
   92 | })
   93 | 
   94 | const getBoxName = (boxId) => {
   95 |   const box = boxes.value.find(b => b.id === boxId)
   96 |   return box ? box.name : boxId
   97 | }
   98 | 
   99 | const getPowerFactorTag = (pf) => {
  100 |   if (pf >= 0.95) return 'success'
  101 |   if (pf >= 0.9) return 'warning'
  102 |   return 'danger'
  103 | }
  104 | 
  105 | const getPowerFactorText = (pf) => {
  106 |   if (pf >= 0.95) return '优秀'
  107 |   if (pf >= 0.9) return '良好'
  108 |   return '需优化'
  109 | }
  110 | </script>
  111 | 
  112 | <style scoped>
  113 | .circuit-stats {
  114 |   display: flex;
  115 |   gap: 20px;
  116 |   margin-bottom: 20px;
  117 | }
  118 | 
  119 | .stat-card {
  120 |   flex: 1;

   21 |       <el-table :data="filteredGroups" border class="group-table" @selection-change="handleSelectionChange">
   22 |         <el-table-column type="selection" width="50"></el-table-column>
   23 |         <el-table-column prop="no" label="No" width="60" align="center"></el-table-column>
   24 |         <el-table-column prop="groupName" label="分组名称" min-width="200"></el-table-column>

   29 |           <template #default="{ row }">
   30 |             <el-button type="primary" size="small" @click="handleBatchOn(row)">全开</el-button>
   31 |             <el-button type="primary" size="small" @click="handleBatchOff(row)">全关</el-button>
   32 |             <el-button type="warning" size="small" @click="handleEdit(row)">修改</el-button>
   33 |             <el-button type="danger" size="small" @click="handleDelete(row)">删除</el-button>

   35 |         </el-table-column>

   44 |           layout="prev, pager, next, jumper, ->, sizes, total"
   45 |         ></el-pagination>
   46 |       </div>
   47 |     </div>
   48 | 
   49 |     <!-- 新增/编辑分组对话框 -->
   50 |     <el-dialog :title="dialogTitle" v-model="showDialog" width="900px" :close-on-click-modal="false">

   52 |         <el-row :gutter="20">
   53 |           <el-col :span="8">

   56 |             </el-form-item>
   57 |           </el-col>

   59 |             <el-form-item label="所属层级" prop="level">

   82 |                 <el-button type="primary" size="small" @click="handleLeftSearch">查询</el-button>
   83 |                 <el-button size="small" @click="handleLeftReset">重置</el-button>
   84 |               </div>

   86 |                 <el-table-column type="selection" width="50"></el-table-column>

   89 |                 <el-table-column prop="centralControl" label="所属集控" min-width="100"></el-table-column>
   90 |               </el-table>

   92 |                 <el-pagination
   93 |                   :current-page="leftPage"
   94 |                   :page-size="10"
   95 |                   :total="leftTotal"
   96 |                   layout="prev, pager, next"
   97 |                   @current-change="handleLeftPageChange"
   98 |                 ></el-pagination>
   99 |               </div>
  100 |             </div>
  101 |           </el-col>
  102 |           <el-col :span="2" class="transfer-buttons">
  103 |             <el-button type="primary" icon="ArrowRight" circle @click="handleMoveRight" :disabled="leftSelected.length === 0"></el-button>
  104 |             <el-button type="primary" icon="ArrowLeft" circle @click="handleMoveLeft" :disabled="rightSelected.length === 0" style="margin-top: 10px;"></el-button>
  105 |           </el-col>
  106 |           <el-col :span="10">
  107 |             <div class="circuit-select">
  108 |               <div class="select-header">
  109 |                 <span class="select-title">已选回路</span>
  110 |                 <el-input v-model="rightSearch" placeholder="请输入回路名称" style="width: 180px; margin-right: 10px;" disabled></el-input>
  111 |               </div>
  112 |               <el-table :data="selectedCircuits" border style="margin-top: 10px;" @selection-change="handleRightSelection" size="small">
  113 |                 <el-table-column type="selection" width="50"></el-table-column>
  114 |                 <el-table-column prop="no" label="No" width="50" align="center"></el-table-column>
  115 |                 <el-table-column prop="circuitName" label="回路名称" min-width="120"></el-table-column>
  116 |                 <el-table-column prop="centralControl" label="所属集控" min-width="100"></el-table-column>
  117 |               </el-table>
  118 |               <div class="empty-tip" v-if="selectedCircuits.length === 0">
  119 |                 暂无数据
  120 |               </div>
  121 |             </div>
  122 |           </el-col>
  123 |         </el-row>
  124 |       </el-form>
  125 |       
  126 |       <template #footer>
  127 |         <el-button @click="handleDialogClose">取消</el-button>
  128 |         <el-button type="primary" @click="handleSubmit">确定</el-button>
  129 |       </template>
  130 |     </el-dialog>
  131 |   </div>
  132 | </template>

  134 | <script setup>
  135 | import { ref, computed } from 'vue'
  136 | import { Search, ArrowRight, ArrowLeft } from '@element-plus/icons-vue'
  137 | import { ElMessage, ElMessageBox } from 'element-plus'
  138 | 
  139 | const currentPage = ref(1)
  140 | const pageSize = ref(15)
  141 | const total = ref(2)
  142 | const searchKeyword = ref('')
  143 | const showDialog = ref(false)
  144 | const isEdit = ref(false)
  145 | const leftPage = ref(1)
  146 | const leftTotal = ref(40)
  147 | const leftSearch = ref('')
  148 | const rightSearch = ref('')
  149 | const selectedRows = ref([])
  150 | const leftSelected = ref([])
  151 | const rightSelected = ref([])
  152 | const groupFormRef = ref(null)
  153 | 
  154 | const groupForm = ref({
  155 |   groupName: '',
  156 |   level: '',
  157 |   remark: ''
  158 | })
  159 | 
  160 | const groupRules = {
  161 |   groupName: [{ required: true, message: '请输入分组名称', trigger: 'blur' }],
  162 |   level: [{ required: true, message: '请选择所属层级', trigger: 'change' }]
  163 | }
  164 | 
  165 | const dialogTitle = computed(() => isEdit.value ? '编辑' : '新增')
  166 | 
  167 | const circuitGroups = ref([
  168 |   {
  169 |     no: 1,
  170 |     groupName: '隔一亮一组',
  171 |     deviceCount: 8,
  172 |     creator: 'test08',
  173 |     remark: '',
  174 |     circuits: [
  175 |       { no: 1, circuitName: '内置回路1', centralControl: '测试128M' },
  176 |       { no: 2, circuitName: '内置回路2', centralControl: '测试128M' },
  177 |       { no: 3, circuitName: '内置回路3', centralControl: '测试128M' },
  178 |       { no: 4, circuitName: '内置回路4', centralControl: '测试128M' },
  179 |       { no: 5, circuitName: '内置回路5', centralControl: '测试128M' },
  180 |       { no: 6, circuitName: '内置回路6', centralControl: '测试128M' },
  181 |       { no: 7, circuitName: '回路1', centralControl: '测试128M' },
  182 |       { no: 8, circuitName: '回路2', centralControl: '测试128M' }
  183 |     ]
  184 |   },
  185 |   {
  186 |     no: 2,
  187 |     groupName: '隔一亮一B组',
  188 |     deviceCount: 0,
  189 |     creator: 'admin',
  190 |     remark: '不可更改',
  191 |     circuits: []
  192 |   }
  193 | ])
  194 | 
  195 | const selectedCircuits = ref([])
  196 | 
  197 | const allCircuits = ref([
  198 |   { no: 1, circuitName: '内置回路1', centralControl: '测试128M' },
  199 |   { no: 2, circuitName: '内置回路2', centralControl: '测试128M' },
  200 |   { no: 3, circuitName: '内置回路3', centralControl: '测试128M' },
  201 |   { no: 4, circuitName: '内置回路4', centralControl: '测试128M' },
  202 |   { no: 5, circuitName: '内置回路5', centralControl: '测试128M' },
  203 |   { no: 6, circuitName: '内置回路6', centralControl: '测试128M' },
  204 |   { no: 7, circuitName: '回路1', centralControl: '测试128M' },
  205 |   { no: 8, circuitName: '回路2', centralControl: '测试128M' },
  206 |   { no: 9, circuitName: '回路3', centralControl: '梅溪湖隧道集控1' },
  207 |   { no: 10, circuitName: '回路4', centralControl: '梅溪湖隧道集控1' },
  208 |   { no: 11, circuitName: '回路5', centralControl: '梅溪湖隧道集控2' },
  209 |   { no: 12, circuitName: '回路6', centralControl: '梅溪湖隧道集控2' }
  210 | ])
  211 | 
  212 | const leftCircuits = computed(() => {
  213 |   const start = (leftPage.value - 1) * 10
  214 |   const end = start + 10
  215 |   let result = allCircuits.value.filter(c => 
  216 |     !selectedCircuits.value.some(sc => sc.no === c.no)
  217 |   )
  218 |   if (leftSearch.value) {
  219 |     result = result.filter(c => 
  220 |       c.circuitName.includes(leftSearch.value) || 
  221 |       c.centralControl.includes(leftSearch.value)
  222 |     )
  223 |   }
  224 |   return result.slice(start, end)
  225 | })
  226 | 
  227 | const filteredGroups = computed(() => {
  228 |   if (!searchKeyword.value) return circuitGroups.value
  229 |   return circuitGroups.value.filter(g => g.groupName.includes(searchKeyword.value))
  230 | })
  231 | 
  232 | const handleSelectionChange = (selection) => {
  233 |   selectedRows.value = selection
  234 | }
  235 | 
  236 | const handleLeftSelection = (selection) => {
  237 |   leftSelected.value = selection
  238 | }
  239 | 
  240 | const handleRightSelection = (selection) => {
  241 |   rightSelected.value = selection
  242 | }
  243 | 
  244 | const handleSearch = () => {
  245 |   ElMessage.success('查询成功')
  246 | }
  247 | 
  248 | const handleReset = () => {
  249 |   searchKeyword.value = ''
  250 |   ElMessage.info('已重置')
  251 | }
  252 | 
  253 | const handleAdd = () => {
  254 |   isEdit.value = false
  255 |   selectedCircuits.value = []
  256 |   groupForm.value = {
  257 |     groupName: '',
  258 |     level: '',
  259 |     remark: ''
  260 |   }
  261 |   showDialog.value = true
  262 | }
  263 | 
  264 | const handleEdit = (row) => {
  265 |   isEdit.value = true
  266 |   groupForm.value = {
  267 |     groupName: row.groupName,
  268 |     level: '1',
  269 |     remark: row.remark
  270 |   }
  271 |   selectedCircuits.value = [...row.circuits]
  272 |   showDialog.value = true
  273 | }
  274 | 
  275 | const handleDelete = (row) => {
  276 |   ElMessageBox.confirm(
  277 |     `确定要删除分组【${row.groupName}】吗？`,
  278 |     '删除确认',
  279 |     {
  280 |       confirmButtonText: '确定',
  281 |       cancelButtonText: '取消',
  282 |       type: 'warning'
  283 |     }
  284 |   ).then(() => {
  285 |     circuitGroups.value = circuitGroups.value.filter(g => g.no !== row.no)
  286 |     total.value--
  287 |     ElMessage.success('删除成功')
  288 |   }).catch(() => {})
  289 | }
  290 | 
  291 | const handleBatchDelete = () => {
  292 |   if (selectedRows.value.length === 0) {
  293 |     ElMessage.warning('请选择要删除的分组')
  294 |     return
  295 |   }
  296 |   ElMessageBox.confirm(
  297 |     `确定要删除选中的 ${selectedRows.value.length} 个分组吗？`,
  298 |     '批量删除确认',
  299 |     {
  300 |       confirmButtonText: '确定',
  301 |       cancelButtonText: '取消',
  302 |       type: 'warning'
  303 |     }
  304 |   ).then(() => {
  305 |     const ids = selectedRows.value.map(r => r.no)
  306 |     circuitGroups.value = circuitGroups.value.filter(g => !ids.includes(g.no))
  307 |     total.value -= selectedRows.value.length
  308 |     selectedRows.value = []
  309 |     ElMessage.success('批量删除成功')
  310 |   }).catch(() => {})
  311 | }
  312 | 
  313 | const handleBatchOn = (row) => {
  314 |   ElMessageBox.confirm(
  315 |     `确定要对分组【${row.groupName}】内的所有回路执行"全开"操作吗？`,
  316 |     '批量控制',
  317 |     {
  318 |       confirmButtonText: '确定',
  319 |       cancelButtonText: '取消',
  320 |       type: 'warning'
  321 |     }
  322 |   ).then(() => {
  323 |     ElMessage.success(`分组【${row.groupName}】内的 ${row.deviceCount} 个回路已全部开启`)
  324 |   }).catch(() => {})
  325 | }
  326 | 
  327 | const handleBatchOff = (row) => {
  328 |   ElMessageBox.confirm(
  329 |     `确定要对分组【${row.groupName}】内的所有回路执行"全关"操作吗？`,
  330 |     '批量控制',
  331 |     {
  332 |       confirmButtonText: '确定',
  333 |       cancelButtonText: '取消',
  334 |       type: 'warning'
  335 |     }
  336 |   ).then(() => {
  337 |     ElMessage.success(`分组【${row.groupName}】内的 ${row.deviceCount} 个回路已全部关闭`)
  338 |   }).catch(() => {})
  339 | }
  340 | 
  341 | const handleMoveRight = () => {
  342 |   if (leftSelected.value.length === 0) {
  343 |     ElMessage.warning('请选择要添加的回路')
  344 |     return
  345 |   }
  346 |   leftSelected.value.forEach(circuit => {
  347 |     if (!selectedCircuits.value.some(c => c.no === circuit.no)) {
  348 |       selectedCircuits.value.push(circuit)
  349 |     }
  350 |   })
  351 |   leftSelected.value = []
  352 |   ElMessage.success('已添加选中的回路')
  353 | }
  354 | 
  355 | const handleMoveLeft = () => {
  356 |   if (rightSelected.value.length === 0) {
  357 |     ElMessage.warning('请选择要移除的回路')
  358 |     return
  359 |   }
  360 |   const ids = rightSelected.value.map(c => c.no)
  361 |   selectedCircuits.value = selectedCircuits.value.filter(c => !ids.includes(c.no))
  362 |   rightSelected.value = []
  363 |   ElMessage.success('已移除选中的回路')
  364 | }
  365 | 
  366 | const handleLeftSearch = () => {
  367 |   leftPage.value = 1
  368 |   ElMessage.success('查询成功')
  369 | }
  370 | 
  371 | const handleLeftReset = () => {
  372 |   leftSearch.value = ''
  373 |   leftPage.value = 1
  374 |   ElMessage.info('已重置')
  375 | }
  376 | 
  377 | const handleLeftPageChange = (page) => {
  378 |   leftPage.value = page
  379 | }
  380 | 
  381 | const handleDialogClose = () => {
  382 |   showDialog.value = false
  383 |   groupFormRef.value?.resetFields()
  384 | }
  385 | 
  386 | const handleSubmit = () => {
  387 |   groupFormRef.value?.validate((valid) => {
  388 |     if (valid) {
  389 |       if (isEdit.value) {
  390 |         const index = circuitGroups.value.findIndex(g => g.no === groupForm.value.no)
  391 |         if (index !== -1) {
  392 |           circuitGroups.value[index].groupName = groupForm.value.groupName
  393 |           circuitGroups.value[index].remark = groupForm.value.remark
  394 |           circuitGroups.value[index].deviceCount = selectedCircuits.value.length
  395 |           circuitGroups.value[index].circuits = [...selectedCircuits.value]
  396 |         }
  397 |         ElMessage.success('修改成功')
  398 |       } else {
  399 |         const newNo = circuitGroups.value.length > 0 ? Math.max(...circuitGroups.value.map(g => g.no)) + 1 : 1
  400 |         circuitGroups.value.push({
  401 |           no: newNo,
  402 |           groupName: groupForm.value.groupName,
  403 |           deviceCount: selectedCircuits.value.length,
  404 |           creator: '管理员',
  405 |           remark: groupForm.value.remark,
  406 |           circuits: [...selectedCircuits.value]
  407 |         })
  408 |         total.value++
  409 |         ElMessage.success('新增成功')
  410 |       }
  411 |       showDialog.value = false
  412 |       groupFormRef.value?.resetFields()
  413 |     }
  414 |   })
  415 | }
  416 | </script>

  302 | const filteredBoxes = computed(() => {
  303 |   let result = boxes.value
  304 |   if (filters.search) {
  305 |     result = result.filter(b => b.code.includes(filters.search) || b.name.includes(filters.search))
  306 |   }
  307 |   if (filters.status) {
  308 |     result = result.filter(b => b.status === filters.status)
  309 |   }
  310 |   if (filters.health) {

  350 | const deleteBox = (row) => {
  351 |   ElMessageBox.confirm(`确定要删除配电柜"${row.name}"吗？`, '提示', {
  352 |     confirmButtonText: '确定',
  353 |     cancelButtonText: '取消',
  354 |     type: 'warning'
  355 |   }).then(() => {
  356 |     const index = boxes.value.findIndex(b => b.id === row.id)
  357 |     if (index > -1) {
  358 |       boxes.value.splice(index, 1)
  359 |       total.value--
  360 |       ElMessage.success('删除成功')
  361 |     }
  362 |   }).catch(() => {})
  363 | }
  364 | 
  365 | const batchDelete = () => {
  366 |   ElMessageBox.confirm(`确定要删除选中的${selectedRows.value.length}个配电柜吗？`, '提示', {
  367 |     confirmButtonText: '确定',
  368 |     cancelButtonText: '取消',
  369 |     type: 'warning'
  370 |   }).then(() => {
  371 |     const selectedIds = selectedRows.value.map(b => b.id)
  372 |     boxes.value = boxes.value.filter(b => !selectedIds.includes(b.id))
  373 |     total.value = boxes.value.length
  374 |     selectedRows.value = []
  375 |     ElMessage.success('批量删除成功')
  376 |   }).catch(() => {})
  377 | }
  378 | 
  379 | const submitForm = () => {
  380 |   formRef.value.validate((valid) => {
  381 |     if (valid) {
  382 |       if (isEdit.value) {
  383 |         ElMessage.success('配电柜修改成功')
  384 |       } else {
  385 |         const newId = Math.max(...boxes.value.map(b => b.id)) + 1
  386 |         boxes.value.push({
  387 |           id: newId,
  388 |           no: boxes.value.length + 1,
  389 |           ...form,
  390 |           status: 'online',
  391 |           health: 'normal',
  392 |           temperature: '-',
  393 |           humidity: '-',
  394 |           lockStatus: 'locked',
  395 |           magneticStatus: 'closed',
  396 |           smokeStatus: 'normal',
  397 |           waterStatus: 'dry'
  398 |         })
  399 |         total.value++
  400 |         ElMessage.success('配电柜添加成功')
  401 |       }
  402 |       showAddDialog.value = false
  403 |     }
  404 |   })
  405 | }

  115 | <script setup>
  116 | import { ref, computed } from 'vue'
  117 | import { Search, ArrowRight, ArrowLeft } from '@element-plus/icons-vue'
  118 | import { ElMessage, ElMessageBox } from 'element-plus'
  119 | 
  120 | const activeTab = ref('lamp')
  121 | const currentPage = ref(1)
  122 | const pageSize = ref(15)
  123 | const total = ref(1)
  124 | const searchKeyword = ref('')
  125 | const showDialog = ref(false)
  126 | const isEdit = ref(false)
  127 | const leftSearch = ref('')
  128 | const rightSearch = ref('')
  129 | const selectedRows = ref([])
  130 | const leftSelected = ref([])
  131 | const rightSelected = ref([])
  132 | const formRef = ref(null)
  133 | 
  134 | const formData = ref({
  135 |   centralControl: ''
  136 | })
  137 | 
  138 | const formRules = {
  139 |   centralControl: [{ required: true, message: '请选择所属集控', trigger: 'change' }]
  140 | }
  141 | 
  142 | const dialogTitle = computed(() => isEdit.value ? '编辑灯控绑定' : '新增灯控绑定')
  143 | 
  144 | const bindData = ref([
  145 |   {
  146 |     no: 1,
  147 |     centralControlName: '梅溪湖隧道集控',
  148 |     centralControlNo: 'ZTJK',
  149 |     bindCount: 2,
  150 |     lampControls: [
  151 |       { no: 1, imei: '867892010000001', lampControlName: '灯控1', lampPoleName: '灯杆001' },
  152 |       { no: 2, imei: '867892010000002', lampControlName: '灯控2', lampPoleName: '灯杆002' }
  153 |     ]
  154 |   }
  155 | ])
  156 | 
  157 | const selectedLampControls = ref([])
  158 | 
  159 | const allLampControls = ref([
  160 |   { no: 1, imei: '867892010000001', lampControlName: '灯控1', lampPoleName: '灯杆001' },
  161 |   { no: 2, imei: '867892010000002', lampControlName: '灯控2', lampPoleName: '灯杆002' },
  162 |   { no: 3, imei: '867892010000003', lampControlName: '灯控3', lampPoleName: '灯杆003' },
  163 |   { no: 4, imei: '867892010000004', lampControlName: '灯控4', lampPoleName: '灯杆004' },
  164 |   { no: 5, imei: '867892010000005', lampControlName: '灯控5', lampPoleName: '灯杆005' },
  165 |   { no: 6, imei: '867892010000006', lampControlName: '灯控6', lampPoleName: '灯杆006' }
  166 | ])
  167 | 
  168 | const filteredData = computed(() => {
  169 |   if (!searchKeyword.value) return bindData.value
  170 |   return bindData.value.filter(item => 
  171 |     item.centralControlName.includes(searchKeyword.value) || 
  172 |     item.centralControlNo.includes(searchKeyword.value)
  173 |   )
  174 | })
  175 | 
  176 | const leftTableData = computed(() => {
  177 |   let result = allLampControls.value.filter(lc => 
  178 |     !selectedLampControls.value.some(slc => slc.imei === lc.imei)
  179 |   )
  180 |   if (leftSearch.value) {
  181 |     result = result.filter(lc => 
  182 |       lc.imei.includes(leftSearch.value) || 
  183 |       lc.lampControlName.includes(leftSearch.value) ||
  184 |       lc.lampPoleName.includes(leftSearch.value)
  185 |     )
  186 |   }
  187 |   return result
  188 | })
  189 | 
  190 | const handleSelectionChange = (selection) => {
  191 |   selectedRows.value = selection
  192 | }
  193 | 
  194 | const handleLeftSelection = (selection) => {
  195 |   leftSelected.value = selection
  196 | }
  197 | 
  198 | const handleRightSelection = (selection) => {
  199 |   rightSelected.value = selection
  200 | }
  201 | 
  202 | const handleSearch = () => {
  203 |   ElMessage.success('查询成功')
  204 | }
  205 | 
  206 | const handleReset = () => {
  207 |   searchKeyword.value = ''
  208 |   ElMessage.info('已重置')
  209 | }
  210 | 
  211 | const handleAdd = () => {
  212 |   isEdit.value = false
  213 |   selectedLampControls.value = []
  214 |   formData.value = {
  215 |     centralControl: ''
  216 |   }
  217 |   showDialog.value = true
  218 | }
  219 | 
  220 | const handleEdit = (row) => {
  221 |   isEdit.value = true
  222 |   formData.value = {
  223 |     centralControl: row.centralControlNo
  224 |   }
  225 |   selectedLampControls.value = [...row.lampControls]
  226 |   showDialog.value = true
  227 | }
  228 | 
  229 | const handleUnbind = (row) => {
  230 |   ElMessageBox.confirm(
  231 |     `确定要对集控【${row.centralControlName}】执行"解绑"操作吗？`,
  232 |     '解绑确认',
  233 |     {
  234 |       confirmButtonText: '确定',
  235 |       cancelButtonText: '取消',
  236 |       type: 'warning'
  237 |     }
  238 |   ).then(() => {
  239 |     const index = bindData.value.findIndex(item => item.no === row.no)
  240 |     if (index !== -1) {
  241 |       bindData.value[index].bindCount = 0
  242 |       bindData.value[index].lampControls = []
  243 |     }
  244 |     ElMessage.success('解绑成功')
  245 |   }).catch(() => {})
  246 | }
  247 | 
  248 | const handleBatchUnbind = () => {
  249 |   if (selectedRows.value.length === 0) {
  250 |     ElMessage.warning('请选择要解绑的集控')
  251 |     return
  252 |   }
  253 |   ElMessageBox.confirm(
  254 |     `确定要对选中的 ${selectedRows.value.length} 个集控执行"解绑"操作吗？`,
  255 |     '批量解绑确认',
  256 |     {
  257 |       confirmButtonText: '确定',
  258 |       cancelButtonText: '取消',
  259 |       type: 'warning'
  260 |     }
  261 |   ).then(() => {
  262 |     selectedRows.value.forEach(row => {
  263 |       const index = bindData.value.findIndex(item => item.no === row.no)
  264 |       if (index !== -1) {
  265 |         bindData.value[index].bindCount = 0
  266 |         bindData.value[index].lampControls = []
  267 |       }
  268 |     })
  269 |     selectedRows.value = []
  270 |     ElMessage.success('批量解绑成功')
  271 |   }).catch(() => {})
  272 | }
  273 | 
  274 | const handleMoveRight = () => {
  275 |   if (leftSelected.value.length === 0) {
  276 |     ElMessage.warning('请选择要添加的灯控')
  277 |     return
  278 |   }
  279 |   leftSelected.value.forEach(lc => {
  280 |     if (!selectedLampControls.value.some(slc => slc.imei === lc.imei)) {
  281 |       selectedLampControls.value.push(lc)
  282 |     }
  283 |   })
  284 |   leftSelected.value = []
  285 |   ElMessage.success('已添加选中的灯控')
  286 | }
  287 | 
  288 | const handleMoveLeft = () => {
  289 |   if (rightSelected.value.length === 0) {
  290 |     ElMessage.warning('请选择要移除的灯控')
  291 |     return
  292 |   }
  293 |   const imeis = rightSelected.value.map(lc => lc.imei)
  294 |   selectedLampControls.value = selectedLampControls.value.filter(lc => !imeis.includes(lc.imei))
  295 |   rightSelected.value = []
  296 |   ElMessage.success('已移除选中的灯控')
  297 | }
  298 | 
  299 | const handleLeftSearch = () => {
  300 |   ElMessage.success('查询成功')
  301 | }
  302 | 
  303 | const handleLeftReset = () => {
  304 |   leftSearch.value = ''
  305 |   ElMessage.info('已重置')
  306 | }
  307 | 
  308 | const handleDialogClose = () => {
  309 |   showDialog.value = false
  310 |   formRef.value?.resetFields()
  311 | }
  312 | 
  313 | const handleSubmit = () => {
  314 |   formRef.value?.validate((valid) => {
  315 |     if (valid) {
  316 |       if (isEdit.value) {
  317 |         const index = bindData.value.findIndex(item => item.centralControlNo === formData.value.centralControl)
  318 |         if (index !== -1) {
  319 |           bindData.value[index].bindCount = selectedLampControls.value.length
  320 |           bindData.value[index].lampControls = [...selectedLampControls.value]
  321 |         }
  322 |         ElMessage.success('修改成功')
  323 |       } else {
  324 |         const centralControlMap = {
  325 |           'ZTJK': '梅溪湖隧道集控',
  326 |           'CS128M': '测试128M',
  327 |           'XDLJK1': '梅溪湖隧道集控1',
  328 |           'XDLJK2': '梅溪湖隧道集控2'
  329 |         }
  330 |         const newNo = bindData.value.length > 0 ? Math.max(...bindData.value.map(item => item.no)) + 1 : 1
  331 |         bindData.value.push({
  332 |           no: newNo,
  333 |           centralControlName: centralControlMap[formData.value.centralControl] || formData.value.centralControl,
  334 |           centralControlNo: formData.value.centralControl,
  335 |           bindCount: selectedLampControls.value.length,
  336 |           lampControls: [...selectedLampControls.value]
  337 |         })
  338 |         total.value++
  339 |         ElMessage.success('新增成功')
  340 |       }
  341 |       showDialog.value = false
  342 |       formRef.value?.resetFields()
  343 |     }
  344 |   })
  345 | }

  154 |

  169 |   { id: 1, cabinetId: 1, name: '断路器', code: 'AL10', lampCount: 0, parentLine: '', controlType: 'breaker', phaseType: 'single', refCurrent: '', ratedPower: '', currentMax: '', currentMin: '', remark: '' }
  170 | ])

  173 |   cabinetId: '',
  174 |   parentLine: '',
  175 |   controlType: '',

  191 |   name: [{ required: true, message: '请输入线路名称', trigger: 'blur' }],

  195 | const filteredCabinets = computed(() => {
  196 |   if (!cabinetSearch.value) return cabinets.value
  197 |   return cabinets.value.filter(c => c.name.includes(cabinetSearch.value) || c.code.includes(cabinetSearch.value))
  198 | })
  199 | 
  200 | const filteredLines = computed(() => {

  207 | }

  212 |     parentLine: '',
  213 |     controlType: '',
  214 |     code: '',
  215 |     name: '',

  229 | }
  230 | 
  231 | const submitForm = () => {
  232 |   formRef.value.validate((valid) => {

  236 |         if (index > -1) {
  237 |           lines.value[index] = { ...lines.value[index], ...form }
  238 |         }
  239 |         ElMessage.success('修改成功')
  240 |       } else {
  241 |         const newId = Math.max(...lines.value.map(l => l.id), 0) + 1
  242 |         lines.value.push({
  243 |           id: newId,
  244 |           ...form,
  245 |           lampCount: 0
  246 |         })
  247 |         ElMessage.success('新增成功')
  248 |       }
  249 |       showAddDialog.value = false
  250 |       isEdit.value = false
  251 |       resetForm()
  252 |     }
  253 |   })
  254 | }

   76 | <script setup>import { ref, computed, onMounted } from 'vue';
   77 | import { ArrowUp, ArrowDown } from '@element-plus/icons-vue';
   78 | import { loadHistoryData, energyStatistics } from '@/data/mockData';
   79 | const icons = { TrendingUp: ArrowUp, TrendingDown: ArrowDown };
   80 | const timeRange = ref('today');
   81 | const voltageChart = ref(null);
   82 | const currentChart = ref(null);
   83 | const powerChart = ref(null);
   84 | const statistics = computed(() => {
   85 |  return energyStatistics[timeRange.value];
   86 | });
   87 | const maxCurrent = computed(() => {
   88 |  return Math.max(...loadHistoryData.current);
   89 | });
   90 | const drawChart = (canvas, data, color, label, unit) => {
   91 |  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
   92 |  const width = canvas.width;
   93 |  const height = canvas.height;
   94 |  const padding = { top: 20, right: 20, bottom: 30, left: 45 };
   95 |  const chartWidth = width - padding.left - padding.right;
   96 |  const chartHeight = height - padding.top - padding.bottom;
   97 |  const maxValue = Math.max(...data) * 1.1;
   98 |  const minValue = Math.min(...data) * 0.9;
   99 |  ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
  100 |  ctx.strokeStyle = '#e8e8e8';
  101 |  ctx.lineWidth = 1;
  102 |  for (let i = 0; i <= 5; i++) {
  103 |  const y = padding.top + (chartHeight / 5) * i;
  104 |  ctx.beginPath();
  105 |  ctx.moveTo(padding.left, y);
  106 |  ctx.lineTo(width - padding.right, y);
  107 |  ctx.stroke();
  108 |  const value = maxValue - ((maxValue - minValue) / 5) * i;
  109 |  ctx.fillStyle = '#999';
  110 |  ctx.font = '11px sans-serif';
  111 |  ctx.textAlign = 'right';
  112 |  ctx.fillText(value.toFixed(1), padding.left - 5, y + 4);
  113 |  }
  114 |  ctx.strokeStyle = '#e8e8e8';
  115 |  for (let i = 0; i < loadHistoryData.labels.length; i++) {
  116 |  const x = padding.left + (chartWidth / (loadHistoryData.labels.length - 1)) * i;
  117 |  ctx.beginPath();
  118 |  ctx.moveTo(x, padding.top);
  119 |  ctx.lineTo(x, height - padding.bottom);
  120 |  ctx.stroke();
  121 |  ctx.fillStyle = '#999';
  122 |  ctx.font = '11px sans-serif';
  123 |  ctx.textAlign = 'center';
  124 |  ctx.fillText(loadHistoryData.labels[i], x, height - 8);
  125 |  }
  126 |  ctx.beginPath();
  127 |  ctx.strokeStyle = color;
  128 |  ctx.lineWidth = 2;
  129 |  ctx.shadowColor = color;
  130 |  ctx.shadowBlur = 5;
  131 |  data.forEach((value, index) => {
  132 |  const x = padding.left + (chartWidth / (data.length - 1)) * index;
  133 |  const y = padding.top + chartHeight - ((value - minValue) / (maxValue - minValue)) * chartHeight;
  134 |  if (index === 0) {
  135 |  ctx.moveTo(x, y);
  136 |  }
  137 |  else {
  138 |  ctx.lineTo(x, y);
  139 |  }
  140 |  });
  141 |  ctx.stroke();
  142 |  ctx.shadowBlur = 0;
  143 |  const lastX = padding.left + chartWidth;
  144 |  const lastY = padding.top + chartHeight - ((data[data.length - 1] - minValue) / (maxValue - minValue)) * chartHeight;
  145 |  ctx.fillStyle = color;
  146 |  ctx.beginPath();
  147 |  ctx.arc(lastX, lastY, 4, 0, Math.PI * 2);
  148 |  ctx.fill();
  149 |  ctx.fillStyle = '#333';
  150 |  ctx.font = '12px sans-serif';
  151 |  ctx.textAlign = 'left';
  152 |  ctx.fillText(`${data[data.length - 1].toFixed(1)}${unit}`, lastX + 8, lastY + 4);
  153 | };
  154 | const drawPowerChart = (canvas) => {
  155 |  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  156 |  const width = canvas.width;
  157 |  const height = canvas.height;
  158 |  const padding = { top: 20, right: 20, bottom: 30, left: 55 };
  159 |  const chartWidth = width - padding.left - padding.right;
  160 |  const chartHeight = height - padding.top - padding.bottom;
  161 |  const powerData = loadHistoryData.power.map(p => p / 1000);
  162 |  const loadData = loadHistoryData.loadPercent;
  163 |  const maxPower = Math.max(...powerData) * 1.1;
  164 |  const maxLoad = 100;
  165 |  ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
  166 |  ctx.strokeStyle = '#e8e8e8';
  167 |  ctx.lineWidth = 1;
  168 |  for (let i = 0; i <= 5; i++) {
  169 |  const y = padding.top + (chartHeight / 5) * i;
  170 |  ctx.beginPath();
  171 |  ctx.moveTo(padding.left, y);
  172 |  ctx.lineTo(width - padding.right, y);
  173 |  ctx.stroke();
  174 |  const powerValue = maxPower - (maxPower / 5) * i;
  175 |  ctx.fillStyle = '#999';
  176 |  ctx.font = '11px sans-serif';
  177 |  ctx.textAlign = 'right';
  178 |  ctx.fillText(powerValue.toFixed(1), padding.left - 5, y + 4);
  179 |  }
  180 |  ctx.fillStyle = '#999';
  181 |  ctx.font = '11px sans-serif';
  182 |  ctx.save();
  183 |  ctx.translate(20, height / 2);
  184 |  ctx.rotate(-Math.PI / 2);
  185 |  ctx.textAlign = 'center';
  186 |  ctx.fillText('功率(kW)', 0, 0);
  187 |  ctx.restore();
  188 |  ctx.strokeStyle = '#e8e8e8';
  189 |  for (let i = 0; i < loadHistoryData.labels.length; i++) {
  190 |  const x = padding.left + (chartWidth / (loadHistoryData.labels.length - 1)) * i;
  191 |  ctx.beginPath();
  192 |  ctx.moveTo(x, padding.top);
  193 |  ctx.lineTo(x, height - padding.bottom);
  194 |  ctx.stroke();
  195 |  ctx.fillStyle = '#999';
  196 |  ctx.font = '11px sans-serif';
  197 |  ctx.textAlign = 'center';
  198 |  ctx.fillText(loadHistoryData.labels[i], x, height - 8);
  199 |  }
  200 |  ctx.beginPath();
  201 |  ctx.strokeStyle = '#1890ff';
  202 |  ctx.lineWidth = 2;
  203 |  ctx.shadowColor = '#1890ff';
  204 |  ctx.shadowBlur = 5;
  205 |  powerData.forEach((value, index) => {
  206 |  const x = padding.left + (chartWidth / (powerData.length - 1)) * index;
  207 |  const y = padding.top + chartHeight - (value / maxPower) * chartHeight;
  208 |  if (index === 0) {
  209 |  ctx.moveTo(x, y);
  210 |  }
  211 |  else {
  212 |  ctx.lineTo(x, y);
  213 |  }
  214 |  });
  215 |  ctx.stroke();
  216 |  ctx.shadowBlur = 0;
  217 |  ctx.beginPath();
  218 |  ctx.strokeStyle = '#52c41a';
  219 |  ctx.lineWidth = 2;
  220 |  ctx.setLineDash([5, 5]);
  221 |  ctx.shadowColor = '#52c41a';
  222 |  ctx.shadowBlur = 3;
  223 |  loadData.forEach((value, index) => {
  224 |  const x = padding.left + (chartWidth / (loadData.length - 1)) * index;
  225 |  const y = padding.top + chartHeight - (value / maxLoad) * chartHeight;
  226 |  if (index === 0) {
  227 |  ctx.moveTo(x, y);
  228 |  }
  229 |  else {
  230 |  ctx.lineTo(x, y);
  231 |  }
  232 |  });
  233 |  ctx.stroke();
  234 |  ctx.setLineDash([]);
  235 |  ctx.shadowBlur = 0;
  236 | };
  237 | const resizeCanvas = (canvas, width, height) => {
  238 |  const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
  239 |  canvas.width = width * dpr;
  240 |  canvas.height = height * dpr;
  241 |  canvas.style.width = width + 'px';
  242 |  canvas.style.height = height + 'px';
  243 |  canvas.getContext('2d').scale(dpr, dpr);
  244 | };
  245 | onMounted(() => {
  246 |  setTimeout(() => {
  247 |  if (voltageChart.value) {
  248 |  resizeCanvas(voltageChart.value, 450, 200);
  249 |  drawChart(voltageChart.value, loadHistoryData.voltage, '#1890ff', '电压', 'V');
  250 |  }
  251 |  if (currentChart.value) {
  252 |  resizeCanvas(currentChart.value, 450, 200);
  253 |  drawChart(currentChart.value, loadHistoryData.current, '#faad14', '电流', 'A');
  254 |  }
  255 |  if (powerChart.value) {
  256 |  resizeCanvas(powerChart.value, 920, 250);
  257 |  drawPowerChart(powerChart.value);
  258 |  }
  259 |  }, 100);
  260 | });
  261 | </script>

  322 | }

  324 | const filteredScenes = computed(() => {
  325 |   let result = scenes.value
  326 |   if (filters.name) {
  327 |     result = result.filter(s => s.name.includes(filters.name))
  328 |   }
  329 |   if (filters.type) {

  331 |   }

  335 | const handleSelectionChange = (selection) => {
  336 |   selectedRows.value = selection
  337 | }

  340 |   currentPage.value = 1
  341 |   ElMessage.success('查询成功')

  344 | const resetFilters = () => {
  345 |   Object.assign(filters, { name: '', type: '' })

  350 |   isEdit.value = false
  351 |   resetSceneForm()
  352 |   showSceneDialog.value = true

  433 |         ElMessage.warning('请至少添加一个定时动作')

  435 |       }

  461 |   }

  140 | 
  141 | const formData = ref({
  142 |   name: '',
  143 |   priority: 'high',
  144 |   executeType: 'always',
  145 |   executeTime: ''
  146 | });

  148 | const rulesData = ref([
  149 |   { id: 1, no: 1, name: '检测有人开', priority: 'high', enabled: true, executeDate: '2025.09.01-2028.10.31', selected: false },
  150 |   { id: 2, no: 2, name: '漏电自动断电', priority: 'high', enabled: true, executeDate: '一直执行', selected: false },
  151 |   { id: 3, no: 3, name: '光照度亮灯', priority: 'high', enabled: true, executeDate: '一直执行', selected: false },
  152 |   { id: 4, no: 4, name: '关回路', priority: 'low', enabled: true, executeDate: '一直执行', selected: false },
  153 |   { id: 5, no: 5, name: '检测无人关', priority: 'low', enabled: true, executeDate: '一直执行', selected: false }
  154 | ]);
  155 | 
  156 | const total = computed(() => rulesData.value.length);
  157 | 
  158 | const filteredRules = computed(() => {
  159 |   let data = [...rulesData.value];
  160 |   if (filterKeyword.value) {
  161 |     const keyword = filterKeyword.value.toLowerCase();
  162 |     data = data.filter(item => item.name.toLowerCase().includes(keyword));
  163 |   }
  164 |   if (filterStatus.value !== '') {
  165 |     const status = filterStatus.value === 'true';
  166 |     data = data.filter(item => item.enabled === status);
  167 |   }
  168 |   if (filterPriority.value) {
  169 |     data = data.filter(item => item.priority === filterPriority.value);
  170 |   }
  171 |   return data.slice((currentPage.value - 1) * pageSize.value, currentPage.value * pageSize.value);
  172 | });
  173 | 
  174 | const handleSearch = () => {
  175 |   currentPage.value = 1;
  176 | };
  177 | 
  178 | const handleReset = () => {
  179 |   filterKeyword.value = '';
  180 |   filterStatus.value = '';
  181 |   filterPriority.value = '';
  182 |   currentPage.value = 1;
  183 | };
  184 |

  188 |

  190 |   showAddDialog.value = true;

  210 |     executeDate: formData.value.executeType === 'always' ? '一直执行' : formData.value.executeTime,
  211 |     selected: false
  212 |   });
  213 |   showAddDialog.value = false;
  214 | };
  215 | 
  216 | const handleEdit = (row) => {
  217 |   alert(`编辑规则：${row.name}`);
  218 | };
  219 | 
  220 | const handleDelete = (row) => {
  221 |   const index = rulesData.value.findIndex(item => item.id === row.id);
  222 |   if (index !== -1) {
  223 |     rulesData.value.splice(index, 1);
  224 |   }
  225 | };
  226 |

  230 |     if (index !== -1) {
  231 |       rulesData.value.splice(index, 1);
  232 |     }
  233 |   });
  234 |   selectedRows.value = [];
  235 | };
  236 |

  238 |   alert(`${rule.name}已${rule.enabled ? '启用' : '禁用'}`);
  239 | };
  240 |

   50 |                   <el-option label="智能主控-站点" value="智能主控-站点" />
   51 |                 </el-select>
   52 |                 <el-select v-model="action.device" placeholder="请选择设备" class="action-select">
   53 |                   <el-option label="展厅隧道灯" value="展厅隧道灯" />
   54 |                   <el-option label="光亚展灯杆" value="光亚展灯杆" />
   55 |                 </el-select>
   56 |                 <div class="delay-group">
   57 |                   <el-input type="number" v-model="action.delay" placeholder="请输入延时时长" class="delay-input" />
   58 |                   <el-select v-model="action.delayUnit" class="delay-unit">
   59 |                     <el-option label="秒" value="秒" />
   60 |                     <el-option label="分" value="分" />
   61 |                     <el-option label="时" value="时" />
   62 |                   </el-select>
   63 |                 </div>
   64 |                 <el-select v-model="action.action" placeholder="请选择动作内容" class="action-select">
   65 |                   <el-option label="开灯" value="开灯" />
   66 |                   <el-option label="关灯" value="关灯" />
   67 |                   <el-option label="调光50%" value="调光50%" />
   68 |                   <el-option label="调光100%" value="调光100%" />
   69 |                 </el-select>
   70 |               </div>
   71 |               <div class="action-controls">
   72 |                 <el-button v-if="index > 0" type="text" @click="moveUp(index)">↑</el-button>
   73 |                 <el-button v-if="index < formData.actions.length - 1" type="text" @click="moveDown(index)">↓</el-button>
   74 |                 <el-button type="text" @click="removeAction(index)">×</el-button>
   75 |               </div>
   76 |             </div>
   77 |           </div>
   78 |         </div>
   79 |       </div>
   80 |     </div>
   81 |   </div>
   82 | </template>
   83 | 
   84 | <script setup>
   85 | import { ref } from 'vue';
   86 | import { Plus } from '@element-plus/icons-vue';
   87 | 
   88 | const formData = ref({
   89 |   name: '',
   90 |   visible: true,
   91 |   sortOrder: 1,
   92 |   actions: [
   93 |     {
   94 |       productType: '',
   95 |       device: '',
   96 |       delay: '',
   97 |       delayUnit: '秒',
   98 |       action: ''
   99 |     }
  100 |   ]
  101 | });
  102 | 
  103 | const addAction = () => {
  104 |   formData.value.actions.push({
  105 |     productType: '',
  106 |     device: '',
  107 |     delay: '',
  108 |     delayUnit: '秒',
  109 |     action: ''
  110 |   });
  111 | };
  112 | 
  113 | const removeAction = (index) => {
  114 |   if (formData.value.actions.length > 1) {
  115 |     formData.value.actions.splice(index, 1);
  116 |   }
  117 | };
  118 | 
  119 | const moveUp = (index) => {
  120 |   if (index > 0) {
  121 |     const temp = formData.value.actions[index];
  122 |     formData.value.actions[index] = formData.value.actions[index - 1];
  123 |     formData.value.actions[index - 1] = temp;
  124 |   }
  125 | };
  126 | 
  127 | const moveDown = (index) => {
  128 |   if (index < formData.value.actions.length - 1) {
  129 |     const temp = formData.value.actions[index];
  130 |     formData.value.actions[index] = formData.value.actions[index + 1];
  131 |     formData.value.actions[index + 1] = temp;
  132 |   }
  133 | };
  134 | 
  135 | const handleSave = () => {
  136 |   if (!formData.value.name) {
  137 |     alert('请输入场景名称');
  138 |     return;
  139 |   }
  140 |   alert('场景保存成功');
  141 | };
  142 | 
  143 | const handleCancel = () => {
  144 |   formData.value = {
  145 |     name: '',
  146 |     visible: true,
  147 |     sortOrder: 1,
  148 |     actions: [
  149 |       {
  150 |         productType: '',
  151 |         device: '',
  152 |         delay: '',
  153 |         delayUnit: '秒',
  154 |         action: ''
  155 |       }
  156 |     ]
  157 |   };
  158 | };
  159 | </script>
  160 |

文件 30/47: views/scene/SceneSchedule.vue
