    1 | <template>
    2 |   <div class="page-container">
    3 |     <div class="page-header">
    4 |       <div class="title">定时场景管理</div>
    5 |       <div class="header-actions">
    6 |         <el-button type="primary" @click="addSchedule">
    7 |           <component :is="icons.Plus" />
    8 |           新增定时
    9 |         </el-button>
   10 |       </div>
   11 |     </div>
   12 |     <el-table :data="schedules" border class="schedule-table">
   13 |       <el-table-column prop="id" label="定时编号" width="100" />
   14 |       <el-table-column prop="name" label="定时名称" />
   15 |       <el-table-column prop="templateName" label="关联场景" width="150" />
   16 |       <el-table-column prop="scheduleType" label="执行类型" width="120">
   17 |         <template #default="scope">
   18 |           <el-tag :type="getTypeTagType(scope.row.scheduleType)">
   19 |             {{ getTypeText(scope.row.scheduleType) }}
   20 |           </el-tag>
   21 |         </template>
   22 |       </el-table-column>
   23 |       <el-table-column prop="time" label="执行时间" width="120" />
   24 |       <el-table-column prop="enabled" label="状态" width="100">
   25 |         <template #default="scope">
   26 |           <el-switch 
   27 |             :value="scope.row.enabled" 
   28 |             @change="toggleEnable(scope.row)"
   29 |             active-color="#13ce66"
   30 |             inactive-color="#ff4949"
   31 |           />
   32 |         </template>
   33 |       </el-table-column>
   34 |       <el-table-column label="操作" width="180">
   35 |         <template #default="scope">
   36 |           <el-button size="small" @click="editSchedule(scope.row)">编辑</el-button>
   37 |           <el-button size="small" type="danger" @click="deleteSchedule(scope.row)">删除</el-button>
   38 |         </template>
   39 |       </el-table-column>
   40 |     </el-table>
   41 |     <el-dialog :title="editDialogTitle" :visible.sync="dialogVisible" width="500px">
   42 |       <el-form :model="formData" label-width="100px">
   43 |         <el-form-item label="定时名称" prop="name">
   44 |           <el-input v-model="formData.name" placeholder="请输入定时名称" />
   45 |         </el-form-item>
   46 |         <el-form-item label="关联场景" prop="templateId">
   47 |           <el-select v-model="formData.templateId" placeholder="请选择场景">
   48 |             <el-option 
   49 |               v-for="template in enabledTemplates" 
   50 |               :key="template.id" 
   51 |               :label="template.name" 
   52 |               :value="template.id" 
   53 |             />
   54 |           </el-select>
   55 |         </el-form-item>
   56 |         <el-form-item label="执行类型" prop="scheduleType">
   57 |           <el-select v-model="formData.scheduleType">
   58 |             <el-option label="每天" value="daily" />
   59 |             <el-option label="周末" value="weekend" />
   60 |             <el-option label="节假日" value="holiday" />
   61 |           </el-select>
   62 |         </el-form-item>
   63 |         <el-form-item label="执行时间" prop="time">
   64 |           <el-time-picker 
   65 |             v-model="formData.time" 
   66 |             format="HH:mm" 
   67 |             placeholder="选择执行时间"
   68 |           />
   69 |         </el-form-item>
   70 |       </el-form>
   71 |       <template #footer>
   72 |         <el-button @click="dialogVisible = false">取消</el-button>
   73 |         <el-button type="primary" @click="saveSchedule">保存</el-button>
   74 |       </template>
   75 |     </el-dialog>
   76 |   </div>
   77 | </template>
   78 | 
   79 | <script setup>
   80 | import { ref, computed } from 'vue'
   81 | import { Plus } from '@element-plus/icons-vue'
   82 | import { scheduledScenes, sceneTemplates } from '@/data/mockData'
   83 | 
   84 | const icons = { Plus }
   85 | const schedules = ref([...scheduledScenes])
   86 | const templates = ref([...sceneTemplates])
   87 | const dialogVisible = ref(false)
   88 | const isEdit = ref(false)
   89 | const formData = ref({
   90 |   id: '',
   91 |   name: '',
   92 |   templateId: '',
   93 |   scheduleType: 'daily',
   94 |   time: '',
   95 |   enabled: true
   96 | })
   97 | 
   98 | const editDialogTitle = computed(() => isEdit.value ? '编辑定时场景' : '新增定时场景')
   99 | 
  100 | const enabledTemplates = computed(() => {
  101 |   return templates.value.filter(t => t.enabled)
  102 | })
  103 | 
  104 | const schedulesWithTemplateName = computed(() => {
  105 |   return schedules.value.map(s => {
  106 |     const template = templates.value.find(t => t.id === s.templateId)
  107 |     return {
  108 |       ...s,
  109 |       templateName: template ? template.name : '未知场景'
  110 |     }
  111 |   })
  112 | })
  113 | 
  114 | const getTypeTagType = (type) => {
  115 |   switch (type) {
  116 |     case 'daily': return 'success'
  117 |     case 'weekend': return 'warning'
  118 |     case 'holiday': return 'info'
  119 |     default: return 'info'
  120 |   }
  121 | }
  122 | 
  123 | const getTypeText = (type) => {
  124 |   switch (type) {
  125 |     case 'daily': return '每天'
  126 |     case 'weekend': return '周末'
  127 |     case 'holiday': return '节假日'
  128 |     default: return type
  129 |   }
  130 | }
  131 | 
  132 | const addSchedule = () => {
  133 |   isEdit.value = false
  134 |   formData.value = {
  135 |     id: '',
  136 |     name: '',
  137 |     templateId: '',
  138 |     scheduleType: 'daily',
  139 |     time: '',
  140 |     enabled: true
  141 |   }
  142 |   dialogVisible.value = true
  143 | }
  144 | 
  145 | const editSchedule = (row) => {
  146 |   isEdit.value = true
  147 |   formData.value = { ...row }
  148 |   dialogVisible.value = true
  149 | }
  150 | 
  151 | const deleteSchedule = (row) => {
  152 |   ElMessageBox.confirm(
  153 |     '确定要删除该定时任务吗？',
  154 |     '提示',
  155 |     {
  156 |       confirmButtonText: '确定',
  157 |       cancelButtonText: '取消',
  158 |       type: 'warning'
  159 |     }
  160 |   ).then(() => {
  161 |     const index = schedules.value.findIndex(s => s.id === row.id)
  162 |     if (index > -1) {
  163 |       schedules.value.splice(index, 1)
  164 |     }
  165 |     ElMessage.success('删除成功')
  166 |   }).catch(() => {
  167 |     ElMessage.info('已取消删除')
  168 |   })
  169 | }
  170 | 
  171 | const toggleEnable = (row) => {
  172 |   row.enabled = !row.enabled
  173 | }
  174 | 
  175 | const saveSchedule = () => {
  176 |   if (!formData.value.name || !formData.value.templateId || !formData.value.time) {
  177 |     ElMessage.warning('请填写完整信息')
  178 |     return
  179 |   }
  180 |   
  181 |   if (isEdit.value) {
  182 |     const index = schedules.value.findIndex(s => s.id === formData.value.id)
  183 |     if (index > -1) {
  184 |       schedules.value[index] = { ...formData.value }
  185 |     }
  186 |     ElMessage.success('修改成功')
  187 |   } else {
  188 |     const newId = 'SCH' + String(schedules.value.length + 1).padStart(3, '0')
  189 |     schedules.value.push({
  190 |       ...formData.value,
  191 |       id: newId
  192 |     })
  193 |     ElMessage.success('新增成功')
  194 |   }
  195 |   dialogVisible.value = false
  196 | }
  197 | </script>
  198 | 
  199 | <style scoped>
  200 | .schedule-table {
  201 |   width: 100%;
  202 | }
  203 | </style>
  204 |

   85 | <script setup>
   86 | import { ref, computed } from 'vue'
   87 | import { Refresh, Sunrise } from '@element-plus/icons-vue'
   88 | import { sceneTemplates } from '@/data/mockData'
   89 | 
   90 | const icons = { Refresh, Lightbulb: Sunrise }
   91 | const templates = ref([...sceneTemplates])
   92 | const confirmDialogVisible = ref(false)
   93 | const pendingScene = ref(null)
   94 | const currentScene = ref(null)
   95 | 
   96 | const triggerHistory = ref([
   97 |   { id: 1, time: '2024-01-15 14:30:22', sceneName: '节能模式', brightness: 50, operator: '管理员', status: 'success' },
   98 |   { id: 2, time: '2024-01-15 10:15:33', sceneName: '节日庆典模式', brightness: 100, operator: '张三', status: 'success' },
   99 |   { id: 3, time: '2024-01-14 22:00:00', sceneName: '深夜模式', brightness: 30, operator: '系统自动', status: 'success' },
  100 |   { id: 4, time: '2024-01-14 18:30:00', sceneName: '日常照明策略', brightness: 100, operator: '系统自动', status: 'success' },
  101 |   { id: 5, time: '2024-01-13 14:20:00', sceneName: '雾霾模式', brightness: 90, operator: '李四', status: 'success' }
  102 | ])
  103 | 
  104 | const enabledTemplates = computed(() => {
  105 |   return templates.value.filter(t => t.enabled)
  106 | })
  107 | 
  108 | const triggerScene = (template) => {
  109 |   pendingScene.value = template
  110 |   confirmDialogVisible.value = true
  111 | }
  112 | 
  113 | const confirmTrigger = () => {
  114 |   if (pendingScene.value) {
  115 |     currentScene.value = {
  116 |       ...pendingScene.value,
  117 |       startTime: new Date().toLocaleString('zh-CN')
  118 |     }
  119 |     triggerHistory.value.unshift({
  120 |       id: Date.now(),
  121 |       time: new Date().toLocaleString('zh-CN'),
  122 |       sceneName: pendingScene.value.name,
  123 |       brightness: pendingScene.value.brightness,
  124 |       operator: '管理员',
  125 |       status: 'success'
  126 |     })
  127 |     ElMessage.success('场景触发成功')
  128 |   }
  129 |   confirmDialogVisible.value = false
  130 | }
  131 | 
  132 | const stopScene = () => {
  133 |   currentScene.value = null
  134 |   ElMessage.info('场景已停止')
  135 | }
  136 | 
  137 | const refreshStatus = () => {
  138 |   ElMessage.success('状态已刷新')
  139 | }
  140 | </script>

  144 | import { ref, computed } from 'vue'

  146 | 
  147 | const filterTunnel = ref('')
  148 | const filterType = ref('')
  149 | const filterStatus = ref('')
  150 | const selectedRows = ref([])
  151 | const currentPage = ref(1)
  152 | const pageSize = ref(15)
  153 | const showBatchDialog = ref(false)
  154 | 
  155 | const summary = ref({
  156 |   total: 48,
  157 |   running: 12,
  158 |   stopped: 32,
  159 |   fault: 4
  160 | })
  161 | 
  162 | const batchForm = ref({
  163 |   type: 'start',
  164 |   windSpeed: 5,
  165 |   executeTime: 'now',
  166 |   scheduleTime: ''
  167 | })
  168 | 
  169 | const ventilationData = ref([
  170 |   { id: 1, tunnelName: '梅溪湖隧道', sectionName: '入口段', name: '射流风机-001', type: '射流风机', status: '运行中', windSpeed: 5.2, frequency: 35, power: 15, runtime: 245 },
  171 |   { id: 2, tunnelName: '梅溪湖隧道', sectionName: '入口段', name: '射流风机-002', type: '射流风机', status: '停止', windSpeed: 0, frequency: 0, power: 0, runtime: 189 },
  172 |   { id: 3, tunnelName: '梅溪湖隧道', sectionName: '基本段', name: '轴流风机-001', type: '轴流风机', status: '运行中', windSpeed: 6.8, frequency: 45, power: 22, runtime: 456 },
  173 |   { id: 4, tunnelName: '梅溪湖隧道', sectionName: '过渡段', name: '射流风机-003', type: '射流风机', status: '故障', windSpeed: 0, frequency: 0, power: 0, runtime: 0 },
  174 |   { id: 5, tunnelName: '梅溪湖隧道', sectionName: '基本段', name: '屋顶风机-001', type: '屋顶风机', status: '运行中', windSpeed: 4.5, frequency: 30, power: 11, runtime: 312 }
  175 | ])
  176 | 
  177 | const total = computed(() => filteredData.value.length)
  178 | 
  179 | const filteredData = computed(() => {
  180 |   let result = ventilationData.value
  181 |   if (filterTunnel.value) {
  182 |     result = result.filter(item => item.tunnelName === filterTunnel.value)
  183 |   }
  184 |   if (filterType.value) {
  185 |     result = result.filter(item => item.type === filterType.value)
  186 |   }
  187 |   if (filterStatus.value) {
  188 |     result = result.filter(item => item.status === filterStatus.value)
  189 |   }
  190 |   return result
  191 | })
  192 | 
  193 | const getStatusType = (status) => {
  194 |   switch (status) {
  195 |     case '运行中':
  196 |       return 'success'
  197 |     case '停止':
  198 |       return 'info'
  199 |     case '故障':
  200 |       return 'danger'
  201 |     default:
  202 |       return ''
  203 |   }
  204 | }
  205 | 
  206 | const handleSearch = () => {
  207 |   currentPage.value = 1
  208 | }
  209 | 
  210 | const handleReset = () => {
  211 |   filterTunnel.value = ''
  212 |   filterType.value = ''
  213 |   filterStatus.value = ''
  214 |   currentPage.value = 1
  215 | }
  216 | 
  217 | const handleSelectionChange = (val) => {
  218 |   selectedRows.value = val
  219 | }
  220 | 
  221 | const handleStart = (row) => {
  222 |   row.status = '运行中'
  223 | }
  224 | 
  225 | const handleStop = (row) => {
  226 |   row.status = '停止'
  227 | }
  228 | 
  229 | const handleAdjust = (row) => {
  230 |   console.log('Adjust:', row)
  231 | }
  232 | 
  233 | const handleBatchControl = () => {
  234 |   if (selectedRows.value.length === 0) {
  235 |     alert('请先选择要控制的设备')
  236 |     return
  237 |   }
  238 |   showBatchDialog.value = true
  239 | }
  240 | 
  241 | const handleBatchConfirm = () => {
  242 |   showBatchDialog.value = false
  243 | }
